## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start Test Suite] --> B[Initialize Validator]
    B --> C{Select Test}
    C --> D[test_validate_put]
    C --> E[test_validate_put_with_missing_id]
    C --> F[test_validate_put_with_invalid_id]
    C --> G[test_validate_put_with_invalid_container_type_id]
    C --> H[test_validate_put_with_missing_fields]
    D --> D1[Create valid PackageContainer]
    D1 --> D2[Set all required fields]
    D2 --> D3[Call validator.validate]
    D3 --> D4[No exception raised - PASS]
    E --> E1[Create PackageContainer with null id]
    E1 --> E2[Call validator.validate]
    E2 --> E3{ValidationError raised?}
    E3 -->|Yes| E4[PASS]
    E3 -->|No| E5[FAIL]
    F --> F1[Create PackageContainer with invalid id]
    F1 --> F2[Call validator.validate]
    F2 --> F3{ValidationError raised?}
    F3 -->|Yes| F4[PASS]
    F3 -->|No| F5[FAIL]
    G --> G1[Create valid PackageContainer]
    G1 --> G2[Set invalid container_type_id]
    G2 --> G3[Call validator.validate]
    G3 --> G4{ValidationError raised?}
    G4 -->|Yes| G5[PASS]
    G4 -->|No| G6[FAIL]
    H --> H1[Test missing all fields]
    H1 --> H2[Test missing 3 fields]
    H2 --> H3[Test missing 2 fields]
    H3 --> H4[Test missing 1 field]
    H4 --> H5{All validations correct?}
    H5 -->|Yes| H6[PASS]
    H5 -->|No| H7[FAIL]
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Test as PutContainerValidatorTest
    participant PC as PackageContainer
    participant Val as PackageContainerValidator
    participant Err as ValidationError
    Test->>Val: __init__() create validator
    Test->>PC: create with valid id
    Test->>PC: set container_type_id
    Test->>PC: set tracking_number
    Test->>PC: set original_unit_of_measurement
    Test->>PC: set weight
    Test->>Val: validate(package_container, "PUT")
    Val-->>Test: success (no exception)
    Test->>PC: create with null id
    Test->>Val: validate(package_container, "PUT")
    Val->>Err: raise ValidationError
    Err-->>Test: ValidationError caught
    Test->>PC: create with invalid id "aaaa"
    Test->>Val: validate(package_container, "PUT")
    Val->>Err: raise ValidationError
    Err-->>Test: ValidationError caught
    Test->>PC: create with valid id
    Test->>PC: set invalid container_type_id
    Test->>Val: validate(package_container, "PUT")
    Val->>Err: raise ValidationError
    Err-->>Test: ValidationError caught
    Test->>PC: create with valid id only
    Test->>Val: validate(package_container, "PUT")
    Val->>Err: raise ValidationError (missing fields)
    Err-->>Test: ValidationError with message
```
